{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 10:18:14","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 10:18:14","title":"Fileless attack protection，fully protect computer security","link":"https://blog.360totalsecurity.com/?p=26240","description":"<img width=\"300\" height=\"195\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2-300x195.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"height: auto; max-width: 300px; width: 100%; margin-bottom: 20px;\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2-300x195.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2-768x500.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2.png 902w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" /><ol>\n<li><strong>What is a fileless attack?</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p>Different from the traditional local disk-based PE executable file attack, fileless attack refers to a malicious attack in which the executable file as a malicious payload runs directly in the memory without being stored on the disk.</p>\n<p>In this way, the virus author avoids directly landing malicious payloads such as PE files on the victim&#8217;s machine, leaving as few traces of behavior on the victim&#8217;s machine as possible, thus avoiding the detection and killing of some traditional security software.</p>\n<p>These fileless attacks are applied to malicious software such as ransomware, mining viruses, remote control Trojans, botnets, etc., and are also favored by more and more APT organizations. With the continuous escalation of network attack and defense, the threat of fileless attack technology has been increasing in the past few years. According to CrowdStrike&#8217;s &#8220;2020 Global Threat Situation Report&#8221; data, in 2019, hackers used modern methods to conduct fileless attacks worldwide. The number exceeds traditional malware attacks.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26160\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"783\" height=\"131\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA1.png 783w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA1-300x50.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA1-768x128.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 783px) 100vw, 783px\" /></a></p>\n<p>However, Users don&#8217;t need to worry too much. Fileless attacks cannot bypass 360 Total Security&#8217;s advanced detection based on behavioral monitoring and other technologies. Through continuous attention and analysis of the latest malicious attack methods, close attention to information on Trojan organization activities, and a large amount of threat intelligence information, 360 Total Security has a complete fileless attack protection solution.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26164\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"902\" height=\"587\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2.png 902w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2-300x195.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA2-768x500.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 902px) 100vw, 902px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>2</strong><strong>．Common fileless attack methods</strong></p>\n<ol>\n<li>1 Fileless attacks based on malicious scripts</li>\n</ol>\n<p>By default, JavaScript, VBScript and PowerShell scripting languages are available on the Windows platform, and the corresponding native applications are: mshta.exe, cscript.exe and powershell.exe.</p>\n<p>For attackers, the advantage of scripts is that they are text files (not binary executable files) and run in the context of an interpreter, which is a trusted component.</p>\n<h3>① JavaScript</h3>\n<p>In 2019, the SideWinder APT organization launched an attack against China. The APT organization used JavaScript memory to execute malicious DLL files compiled by .net. The attacker first uses the Office remote code execution vulnerability (cve-2017-11882) to decrypt and execute the JavaScript script, and then executes the Trojan load through the JavaScript script memory. The main attack chain is shown in the following figure:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26232\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"681\" height=\"189\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA3.png 681w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA3-300x83.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 681px) 100vw, 681px\" /></a></p>\n<h3>② VBScript and Powershell</h3>\n<p>njRAT, also known as Bladabindi or Njw0rm, is a remote access trojan (RAT, remote access trojan), which can control the infected system and provide a series of remote control functions for remote attackers. With the upgrading of offensive and defensive technology, njRAT remote control also began to join fileless attack technology. In an attack event captured by 360 Security Center where njRAT was spread by a download site, the attacker used VBScript plus a powershell script to achieve a fileless attack. The main attack chain is shown in the following figure:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26244\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"869\" height=\"157\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA4.png 869w, 869px\" /></a></p>\n<p>A malicious script named system32.vbs will call powershell to access malicious files hosted on Microsooft Onedrive, and copy itself to the startup directory to achieve local persistence:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26176\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA5.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"636\" height=\"192\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA5.png 636w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA5-300x91.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 636px) 100vw, 636px\" /></a></p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>The powershell parameters after Base64 decryption are as follows, and the function is to download and run the obfuscated njRat:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA00.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26248\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA00.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"784\" height=\"61\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA00.png 784w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA00-300x23.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA00-768x60.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 784px) 100vw, 784px\" /></a></p>\n<p>1.2 Fileless attacks based on malicious documents</p>\n<p>In fileless attacks based on malicious documents, attackers often deliver malicious text documents in the form of email attachments, and use social engineering to induce target users to execute the shellcode or macro script in the document.</p>\n<p>First of all, the diversity of Microsoft office document functions not only provides convenience to users, but also presents more possibilities for attackers to exploit vulnerabilities. Attackers usually use vulnerabilities to execute embedded malicious shellcode commands, and use the shellcode as a springboard to achieve further attacks. For example, the SideWinder APT organization mentioned above uses the Office remote code execution vulnerability (CVE-2017-11882).</p>\n<p>Secondly, the VBA macros supported by Microsoft office documents also provide an opportunity for attackers. Attackers will use traditional security software to distinguish the malicious weakness of macro instructions, and perform actions such as downloading malicious code by running office macros.</p>\n<p>Finally, using the defects of loading additional templates for Word documents in Microsoft Office to launch malicious request template injection attacks is also a common fileless attack based on malicious documents.</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>① MICROSOFT OFFICE macro</p>\n<p>The Ursnif banking Trojan has used fileless attacks based on office macros. Ursnif is a frequently active banking Trojan, also known as the Gozi banking Trojan. It is a variant of the Gozi-ISFB banking Trojan. Since the source code of the Trojan was leaked in 2014, attackers have been upgrading Ursnif features. In the Ursnif banking Trojan&#8217;s attack on Italy in early 2019, a fileless attack based on office macros was used. The main attack chain is shown in the following figure:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA111.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26252\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA111.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"748\" height=\"237\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA111.png 748w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA111-300x95.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 748px) 100vw, 748px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The Excel file with malicious macro will display &#8220;error&#8221; when it is opened, so as to induce the user to enable the macro. Once the user chooses to enable the macro, the macro instruction will be further decrypted to execute the powershell script, download the exe file and execute it, the exe file The role of is as a downloader of the final load.</p>\n<p>The macro screenshot is as follows:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA7.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26184\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA7.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"577\" height=\"497\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA7.png 577w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA7-300x258.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 577px) 100vw, 577px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The decrypted powershell command is as follows:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA8.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26188\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA8.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1108\" height=\"365\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA8.png 1108w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA8-300x99.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA8-768x253.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA8-1024x337.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1108px) 100vw, 1108px\" /></a></p>\n<ul>\n<li>WORD template injection</li>\n</ul>\n<p>At the beginning of 2020, the Gamaredon APT organization used the word template injection method to implement attacks against European countries and other countries. Gamaredon is an APT organization that first appeared in 2013, mainly for cyber espionage against Ukraine. In 2017, the organization was exposed to attacks against Ukraine and was named the Gamaredon group for the first time.</p>\n<p>At the beginning of 2020, Gamaredon carried out an attack based on word template injection with Covid-19 related emails. The attack delivers a word document file as an email attachment. When the document is opened, the attacker will use template injection to download a document template containing malicious macro code from the Internet. The macro will further request a payload from the C&#38;C server. By the way, from the perspective of the function of the vbs script, this attack by the Gamaredon organization will eventually lead to the landing of the payload, but this does not prevent us from studying what word template injection technology can do in fileless attacks. effect. The main attack chain of Gamaredon&#8217;s attack is shown below:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA222.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full final load from the server:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA13.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26204\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA13.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"613\" height=\"764\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA13.png 613w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA13-241x300.png 241w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 613px) 100vw, 613px\" /></a></p>\n<h2>1.3 LOLBins</h2>\n<p>The term &#8220;Living off the land&#8221; (LOL) was first proposed by Christopher Campbell and Matt Graeber at the DerbyCon hacker conference in 2013 to summarize the use of credible, pre-installed system tools to spread malware. Finally, Philip Goh The concept of LOLBins (&#8220;Living Off the Land Binaries&#8221;) is further put forward to represent the Windows binary files used in this technology, such as regsvr32.exe, rundll32.exe, certutil.exe, schtasks.exe, wmic.exe, etc. System native tools fall into this category.</p>\n<p>Astaroth Trojan is a kind of information stealing Trojan. It steals various sensitive information and sends it back to the Trojan C&#38;C server. A new variant of the Astaroth Trojan revealed in 2019, its attack chain includes the abuse of LOLBins.</p>\n<p>The Trojan first delivers a phishing email containing a malicious link. If the user clicks on the link in the email, it will download a ZIP file with anLNK file. When the LNK file with the inductive name is clicked, the LNK file will run the bat script, and the bat script will call wmic.exe to download the XLS file with the obfuscated JavaScript script. The JavaScript script will use Bitsadmin.exe to download the disguise After passing the payload, use Certutil.exe to decrypt the payload, and use Regsvr32 combined with process injection technology to run the real payload. The main attack chain is shown below:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA14.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26208\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA14.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"479\" height=\"498\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA14.png 479w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA14-289x300.png 289w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 479px) 100vw, 479px\" /></a></p>\n<ol start=\"3\">\n<li><strong>360 TOTAL SECURITY comprehensive protection against file-free attack threats</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p>360 Total Security provides security solutions against fileless attacks, protecting personal computers by using open, proactive and intelligently driven methods. The new 360 Total Security integrates technologies such as behavior monitoring, terminal enhancement, and cloud services based on big data, which can effectively protect against various fileless attacks.</p>\n<p>Endpoint enhancement: 360 Total Security&#8217;s advanced endpoint security solution provides basic defense measures for personal terminals, such as vulnerability repair, memory scanning, system critical area scanning, firewall and URL filtering.</p>\n<p>Behavior monitoring: 360 Total Security&#8217;s behavior monitoring engine is based on behavior detection technology, which monitors various processes and system events in operation, and can effectively detect and block fileless attack threats during the execution phase.</p>\n<p>Big data-based cloud service: 360 Total Security uses big data-based cloud service technology to provide accurate, real-time and intelligent protection, able to quickly identify new threats, enhance standard real-time protection, and bring the best security protection.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/FA15.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26212\" access tool njRAT is active. Compared with the early infection of the njRAT Trojan&#8217;s executable program landing method, the Trojan uses scripts such as powershell to implement executable program memory execution to complete data theft and other malicious behaviors. , Added more complicated code obfuscation and anti-analysis methods. And through the analysis of the related files of the njRAT Trojan C&#38;C server, it can be found that the njRAT load adopts a variety of different delivery methods.</p>\n<p>njRAT, also known as Bladabindi or Njw0rm, is a remote access trojan (RAT, remote access trojan), which can control the infected system and provide a series of remote control functions for remote attackers.</p>\n<p>The Trojan is mainly spread through download sites, and uses a variety of different njRAT payload delivery methods.</p>\n<p>First, package the Trojan horse script and normal software and place them on some websites such as irregular download sites. When users download and run the installation package, while the normal software is installed, the njRAT also gets the first opportunity to invade the victim&#8217;s machine. . At the same time, through the analysis of the files associated with the Trojan C&#38;C server address 95.211.239.201, it can also be found that the njRAT payload has adopted various delivery methods as described below to infect the victim&#8217;s machine.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25960\" loading</strong></p>\n<p>（1）cnews.vbs</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25964\" start=\"3\">\n<li><strong> The puppet process injects and loads the RAT</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p>The way to load njRAT by injecting a puppet process is still implemented by using scripts such as powershell in the early stage. The trojan horse visits hxxps://2u.pw/3aX42 through powershell and download the powershell script VN1.jpg disguised as a picture first, and then this script is responsible for loading the DelPhi version of the RAT by way of puppet process injection to steal information.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25996\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1024\" height=\"118\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-2.png 1024w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-2-300x35.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-2-768x89.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></a></p>\n<p>VN1.jpg contains the data of two PE files. The $Cli555 variable contains the data of the dll whose original file name is &#8220;WindowsFormsApplication42.dll&#8221;. This dll is responsible for loading the Delphi version of the RAT by way of puppet process injection, which is the value of $Cli444. The RAT file data contained in the variable.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11-1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26000\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1009\" height=\"112\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11-1.png 1009w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11-1-300x33.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11-1-768x85.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1009px) 100vw, 1009px\" /></a></p>\n<p>&#8220;WindowsFormsApplication42.dll&#8221; will inject the Delphi version of the RAT into the MSBuild.exe process by writing memory and setting the context of the thread.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26004\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"586\" height=\"557\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-1.png 586w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-1-300x285.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 586px) 100vw, 586px\" /></a></p>\n<p>It is worth noting that the powershell script used by the Trojan horse author to inject the puppet process (such as VN1.jpg above) is also full of tricks and has multiple versions.</p>\n<p>For example, the powershell script in the &#8220;vv2.txt&#8221; file, one of the advanced versions, confuses the PE file data, and uses aspnet_compiler.exe as the target puppet process to be injected.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26008\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1154\" height=\"240\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1.png 1154w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1-300x62.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1-768x160.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1-1024x213.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1154px) 100vw, 1154px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Another example is the powershell script in another advanced version of the &#8220;wwe.png&#8221; For example, detect and counter common analysis tools such as VmWare, VirtualBox, Fiddler, DnSpy, Process Monitor, HttpDebugger, etc.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-26020\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"558\" height=\"669\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-1.png 558w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-1-250x300.png 250w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 558px) 100vw, 558px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>njRAT detailed features</strong></p>\n<p>The Trojan C&#38;C server (95.211.239.201) is associated with multiple different versions of njRAT, with basically the same functions, similar to the Delphi version of RAT, and the information stolen by these RATs will be returned to the server address 95.211.239.201.</p>\n<p>Here is a detailed introduction to the functions in njRAT. Its functions mainly include obtaining disk volume serial number, computer name and user name, Trojan file update date, operating system full name, system service pack version, CPU processor architecture (32-bit/64 Bit), retrieve the capture driver to determine whether the camera exists, obtain information such as the current window title, and process and execute C&#38;C 582px\" /></a></p>\n<ol start=\"5\">\n<li><strong> Summary</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p>Compared with previous similar Trojan horses, this variant of njRAT is mainly updated with diversified load delivery methods relying on scripts such as powershell, and code obfuscation and analysis countermeasures relying on open source projects.</p>\n<p>First of all, the powerful features of PowerShell, while providing convenience to users, also open the door to many criminals. More and more attackers are beginning to use PowerShell to take advantage, download malicious files through powershell, or execute malicious code in memory to achieve intangible file attacks, etc., so as to avoid some anti-virus detection and bring serious problems to enterprises and individuals. Security threats.</p>\n<p>Secondly, in this example attack, the Trojan horse author used a code obfuscation and anti-analysis project that was open sourced on github at the beginning of this year. This shows that the Trojan horse author has continued to pay attention to malicious tools and code utilization, and has become more frequent. Malicious open source projects are exploited. At the same time, it is worth noting that cloud-based storage platforms have long been abused by attackers, from hosting malicious files to delivering malicious software, and even using them as part of a command and control (C&#38;C) architecture. In this case, the Trojan author used Microsoft OneDrive to host his malicious powershell script.</p>\n<p>At the same time, we noticed that, as one of the poisonous installation packages of njRAT&#8217;s original carrier, its symbolic path name is: C:\\Users\\chirats\\Desktop\\news\\دمج شغال\\sS\\sS\\obj\\Debug\\sS.pdb, Based on the Arabic &#8220;دمج شغال&#8221; in the path, we speculate that the Trojan horse author may come from a country in the Middle East or North Africa.</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>Security Advice:</p>\n<ol>\n<li>Go to http://www.360totalsecurity.com/ to download and install 360 Total Security which can effectively protect against similar virus threats;</li>\n<li>Improve personal network security awareness. It is recommended to download and install software from official channels. For unfamiliar software blocked by 360 Total Security, do not continue to run and add trust;</li>\n<li>According to the usage of powershell, modify the execution strategy of the local powershell, such as modifying the execution strategy to prohibit running any scripts or run scripts with trusted digital signatures.</li>\n</ol>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>Md5:</p>\n<p>df291350b793205204e2e305af9eb1fb</p>\n<p>4563f44a47220396760ffec3aabceead</p>\n<p>2094f262e378273f08f836699953605f</p>\n<p>d7668d89577fec1912418da082c4c5c3</p>\n<p>13180caea7565ed8cde3e2b3a6c59313</p>\n<p>f9747a5cdd3f329572e5945a80fe11e7</p>\n<p>e1eda3e6f6b204d486b6a97026c9feae</p>\n<p>041e3fe888230e1dda9949a8a741054e</p>\n<p>57445041f7a1e57da92e858fc3efeabe</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>URLS:</p>\n<p>hxxps://2u.pw/3aX42</p>\n<p>https://2u.pw/zIH2Z</p>\n<p>hxxps://2u.pw/RxSsS</p>\n<p>hxxps://dl.dropboxusercontent.com/s/m6q5dhmjpfxes94/ps2.txt</p>\n<p>hxxps://dl.dropboxusercontent.com/s/lpoe7mktxd3zi1r/ps1.txt</p>\n<p>hxxps://onedrive.live.com/download?cid=673EE675C72FC07C&#38;resid=673EE675C72FC07C%21132&#38;authkey=AIMSMV6FkJfJyCI</p>\n<p>hxxps://onedrive.live.com/download?cid=F8F1505E1B355606&#38;resid=F8F1505E1B355606!1388&#38;authkey=AM1NXoCYykwqLFA</p>\n<p>hxxps://onedrive.live.com/Download?cid=1999A3757EF7BB87&#38;resid=1999A3757EF7BB87%21126&#38;authkey=ANPgrMDyhVNehZI</p>\n<p>hxxp://www.asmreekasounds.com/upfiles/up_down/1fe352263637133298954dbac2a7821a.mp3</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>The After in-depth analysis, it was found that this was another &#8220;poisoning&#8221; operation by the hacker group &#8220;Oldpanther&#8221;.</p>\n<p>We found that the organization began active at the end of May in this year, with supply chain attacks, the infectious virus Peviru lurking in the Chinese programming language compilation environment was issued, causing all programs compiled by users to escape infection. 360 Total Security completed the interception and killing of the virus immediately after its discovery.</p>\n<p>Nowdays, the revitalized &#8220;Oldpanther&#8221; come out again, using the previously deployed virus module to deliver the new ransomware Panther, which has once again set off a wave of evil in cyberspace.</p>\n<p>However, users do not need to worry a lot. 360 Total Security has supported the decryption for Panther ransomware. Infected users can download and install the 360 decryption tools and protect personal data and property safety.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25652\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1582\" height=\"1048\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-2.png 1582w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-2-300x199.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-2-768x509.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-2-1024x678.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1582px) 100vw, 1582px\" /></a></p>\n<p>At the end of May, 360 Security Center found that the virus was aimed at the source of the compiled program, and by sneaking into the Chinese programming language installation program and other related modules, it traversed the entire network, causing many Chinese recruiting equipment to become A &#8220;puppet&#8221; FlyBox&#8221; and display the following bullet box titled &#8220;Your Files Encrypted&#8221;, the text in the bullet box describes the ransomware threat at 72 Remit to the Bitcoin wallet address &#8220;1MkdmGEu9vTjqRYrFp4TWbsSK9SjECTbGD&#8221; with a value of USD 80 within hours, and send a ransom payment certificate to the virus author mailbox mykeyhelp@protonmail.com, and threaten the victim to obtain a decryption key and decrypt the victim&#8217;s file. However, as of now, the wallet has not received any payment.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25524\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"951\" height=\"812\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.2.png 951w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.2-300x256.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.2-768x656.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 951px) 100vw, 951px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Figure 1 YourFilesEncrypted virus box blackmails Bitcoin</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25528\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"481\" height=\"92\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.3.png 481w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.3-300x57.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 481px) 100vw, 481px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Figure 2 The encrypted file has the file extension &#8220;.FlyBox&#8221;</p>\n<p>The virus first decompresses and runs the main body of the ransomware Flonwd.exe from the resource section of the confused C# program. Flonwd.exe is an executable file packaged by pyinstaller, which creates _MEIxxxxx (_MEI+random number) in the %temp% directory Folder, unzip and release files such as the python module used to encrypt ransomware, and then use the AES and RSA algorithms to encrypt the victim files through the python module.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.4.png\"><img form of a hoax has appeared on the network. In view of the encrypted file suffix of the virus is named &#8220;.flowEncryption&#8221;, we named it &#8220;flowEncryption file encryption virus&#8221;.</p>\n<p>After encrypting the victim&#8217;s files, the virus does not ask the ransom victim for ransom, and maliciously encrypts the victim&#8217;s files purely in a mischievous manner.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25756\" 812px\" /></a></p>\n<p>After the flowEncryption virus runs, it will encrypt the file and add the encrypted file with the suffix &#8220;.flowEncryption&#8221;, but it will not blackmail the AutoIt script, which uses Microsoft cryptographic service providers (CSP) to encrypt the victim file and add the corresponding suffix name.</p>\n<p>According to the content of the decompiled .au3 script file, it can be found that the file encryption function of the virus is copied from the source code for the CTF network security contest published on the github by the academic team named &#8220;Revers3c&#8221;. Virus authors use this source code to encrypt files without extorting the victim to satisfy their mischievous mentality of teasing others for their own pleasure.</p>\n<p>The virus encrypts files in various subfolders in the %Userprofile% directory, as well as mobile hard disk files.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25764\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"685\" height=\"767\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.3.png 685w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.3-268x300.png 268w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 685px) 100vw, 685px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The virus encrypts files through the CSP encryption service. First call CryptAcquireContext, use the CSP encryption algorithm based on RSA+AES encryption type to obtain the handle of the specified CSP key container, and call CryptDeriveKey to generate the session key through the AES256 encryption algorithm. In addition to encryption-related function functions, the virus author also added file operations, array operations, and other related functions to the code to confuse the audition. In fact, these functions have not been called.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25768\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1357\" height=\"323\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.4.png 1357w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.4-300x71.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.4-768x183.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.4-1024x244.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1357px) 100vw, 1357px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25772\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.5.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"824\" height=\"803\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.5.png 824w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.5-300x292.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.5-768x748.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 824px) 100vw, 824px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>Security Advices</strong></p>\n<p>1.Go to http://www.360totalsecurity.com/ to download and install 360 Total Security to effectively protect against similar virus threats;</p>\n<p>2.To improve personal network security awareness, it is recommended to download and install software from official channels such as the software official website. Recently, 360 Security Brain has detected an XMRig Monero variant miner, in the form of a camouflage system WMI service, many countries around the world have &#8220;successfully captured&#8221; since 2018.</p>\n<p>Not only is the infection path of the installation program of the mining Trojan very concealed, but the persistence method is also complex and multi-end, so that ordinary users can not be protected at all; while the Trojan horse bat script is downloaded to the malicious file of the host computer, even with the mining program to read and write MSR The WinRing0x64.sys register and the open source file ps2exe that converts the powershell script into an executable file for the Windows platform are also listed, which means that once the computer is unfortunately recruited, it is difficult to get out of the way.</p>\n<p>At present, 360 Total Security can effectively intercept and kill the mining Trojan. It first calls the cmd process to run the font.bat script, downloads an adapted open source Monero coin miner bat installation script from the server, and randomly names temporary files tmpxxxx.tmp.bat, and then call powershell to run the script to install the mining machine, and finally achieve resident on the host computer.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25364\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"242\" height=\"480\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2.png 242w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-151x300.png 151w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 242px) 100vw, 242px\" /></a><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25368\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"977\" height=\"119\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3.png 977w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3-300x37.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3-768x94.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 977px) 100vw, 977px\" /></a></p>\n<p>This script is adapted from the open source Monero coin miner installation script. directory, and sets the Trojan file attributes to system file attributes and hidden file attributes to hide itself as much as possible, and Add a registry service item named compiler, register the windows service registration tool nssm as a service, and then call the mining program WMIProviderHost from nssm in the form of parameters, so as to achieve the purpose of the mining Trojan staying on the host computer.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25380\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1165\" height=\"500\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6.png 1165w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-300x129.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-768x330.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-1024x439.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1165px) 100vw, 1165px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The mining main body of the Trojan is WMIProviderHost.exe in the &#8220;%SYSTEMROOT%\\SysWOW64\\WMIScriptingAPI&#8221; directory. This program describes the file information as a system file (WMIProviderHost) in an attempt to confuse the host. In fact, it is an XMRig Monero mining Trojan that dominates the user&#8217;s computer resources. The Trojan will read the mining pool configuration file srnany.exe in the same directory to mine.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25384\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"787\" height=\"430\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7.png 787w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-300x164.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-768x420.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 787px) 100vw, 787px\" /></a></p>\n<p>By querying the wallet address in the configuration file, you can see that under the total computing power of the currently infected computer, the daily income of the wallet is 0.2258XMR/14.71 USD.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25388\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1511\" height=\"528\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8.png 1511w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-300x105.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-768x268.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-1024x358.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1511px) 100vw, 1511px\" /></a></p>\n<p>In the unzipped file of the mining file placed by the Trojan author on github, you can also see the NSIS miner installer tool nssy.exe, the windows service registration tool nssm.exe, and you can see some tools that the author will prepare to use later. https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Blog封面01.png 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" /><p>In recent years, the spread of ransomware has become increasingly severe, thousands of servers and databases around the world have been invaded and destroyed. Among them, the Phobos ransomware virus family is notorious for being evil all year round.</p>\n<p>The Phobos ransomware first appeared in December 2018, and it was named after the suffix Phobos was added to encrypted files.</p>\n<p>Recently, 360 Security Center has detected that a new variant of the Phobos ransomware virus appeared on the network. The virus uses software such as system activation tools as a carrier to induce users to download and install, steal the user’s machine information, and further pass the Trojan C&#38;C server Download encryption ransomware related programs and implement Bitcoin ransomware. In just over a week, the variant has spread to more than ten countries.</p>\n<p>Currently, 360 Total Security can effectively intercept and kill the ransomware variant. It is recommended that users download and install the latest version of 360 Total Security as soon as possible to fully protect personal privacy and property security.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25824\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"580\" height=\"381\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-4.png 580w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/1-4-300x197.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 580px) 100vw, 580px\" /></a></p>\n<p>According to 360 Security Center Monitoring, the ransomware variant uses software such as system activation tools as a breakthrough.Once the user is induced to download and run, disguised as the first layer of &#8220;sheepskin&#8221; powershell script, another powershell script will be downloaded and executed pps.ps1, pps.ps1 will decrypt and release the base64-encrypted exe file data to %userprofile% In the directory and loaded, the exe implements the theft of the victim’s computer information and further downloads the encrypted ransom related files through the Trojan C&#38;C server.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25828\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1224\" height=\"177\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-4.png 1224w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-4-300x43.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-4-768x111.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/2-4-1024x148.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1224px) 100vw, 1224px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25832\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"613\" height=\"503\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3-4.png 613w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/3-4-300x246.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 613px) 100vw, 613px\" /></a></p>\n<p>After the file is encrypted, the Phobos ransomware variant will add a specific suffix named id[XXXXXXXX-2275].[helprecover@foxmail.com].help, where &#8220;XXXXXXXX&#8221; is the disk serial number.</p>\n<p>At the same time, it will release files named info.hta and info.txt as blackmail letters in the desktop directory and disk root directory of the victim&#8217;s computer. By calling the info.hta program with the same text content as info.txt, the box titled &#8220;All your files have been encrypted&#8221; will inform the victim of the virus author&#8217;s contact information and the Bitcoin ransom payment method.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/4-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25836\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/4-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1316\" height=\"598\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/4-4.png 1316w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/4-4-300x136.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/4-4-768x349.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/4-4-1024x465.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1316px) 100vw, 1316px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/5-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25840\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/5-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1316\" height=\"432\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/5-4.png 1316w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/5-4-300x98.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/5-4-768x252.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/5-4-1024x336.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1316px) 100vw, 1316px\" /></a></p>\n<p>According to the pps.ps1 script, the time stamp of the release of the virus exe program is 2020/7/12. It can be seen that in the short period of more than one week since the time stamp, the ransomware variant has spread and infected more than ten countries.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25844\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1316\" height=\"862\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-4.png 1316w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-4-300x197.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-4-768x503.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/6-4-1024x671.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1316px) 100vw, 1316px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Compared with the previous version, the Phobos ransomware variant has been upgraded in many aspects, such as camouflaging the encrypted ransomware function module, bypassing the security protection mechanism, and local persistence. After in-depth analysis, 360 Security Center reproduced the &#8220;five sins&#8221; of the rampant evil of the ransomware variant.</p>\n<p>When the user downloads and executes the exe file in the %userprofile% directory and decrypts and releases it by powershell, it will further download the executable program zeVrk.exe and other files used for file encryption from the Trojan server to complete the encryption ransom behavior.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25848\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"697\" height=\"1073\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-4.png 697w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-4-195x300.png 195w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/7-4-665x1024.png 665w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 697px) 100vw, 697px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The virus first uses SilentCleanup in the scheduled task to bypass UAC, and then obtains the Trojan horse program with the original file name zeVrk.exe from the Trojan server.</p>\n<p>The Trojan horse program will extract and decrypt the base64-encrypted dll data named &#8220;AndroidStudio.dll&#8221; from the resource section, call its export function StartGame(), and then continue to extract the encrypted file data from the resource section of the dll, and then transfer it Decompress and XOR decrypt, restore to the exe file data responsible for the encryption and ransom function, and then load the exe. After &#8220;take off&#8221; the disguised &#8220;sheepskin&#8221; decrypted and loaded in the two-layer resource segment, the exe will complete the substantial file encryption operation.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25928\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-5.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1316\" height=\"664\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-5.png 1316w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-5-300x151.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-5-768x388.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/8-5-1024x517.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1316px) 100vw, 1316px\" /></a></p>\n<p>zeVrk.exe decrypts the AndroidStudio.dll file data of the resource segment and calls its export function StartGame()<a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/9-1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25932\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/9-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1316\" height=\"182\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/9-1.png 1316w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/9-1-300x41.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/9-1-768x106.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/9-1-1024x142.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1316px) 100vw, 1316px\" /></a></p>\n<p>AndroidStudio.dll! StartGame decompresses, decrypts and loads the exe responsible for file encryption</p>\n<p>Once the virus variant invades successfully, it will first steal hardware information such as the CPU model, sound card and graphics card on the target computer, as well as user information such as country, IP address, and installed software, and write this information into the &#8220;system.txt&#8221; file; at the same time It will also try to obtain the local account password information and write it into the &#8220;password.txt&#8221; file; it will also name the current screenshot obtained as &#8220;screenshot.jpg&#8221;.</p>\n<p>Then, it will package these three files as compressed files and send them back to the Trojan horse server and delete the local compressed package files. These stolen user information are likely to be the first to further potential attacks by the Phobos family in the future.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25936\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"632\" height=\"701\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-1.png 632w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/10-1-270x300.png 270w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 632px) 100vw, 632px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25868\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"319\" height=\"124\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11.png 319w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/11-300x117.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 319px) 100vw, 319px\" /></a></p>\n<p>This virus variant also downloads a program with the original file name &#8220;Disable-Windows-Defender.exe&#8221; through the Trojan horse server to disable various functions of Windows Defender.</p>\n<p>The method includes: modify the registry to turn off Windows Defender real-time protection and other functions, call powershell to execute the &#8220;Get-MpPreference -verbose&#8221; command to check the current Windows Defender settings, and try to turn off the specified Windows Defender function.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25872\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1302\" height=\"206\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12.png 1302w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-300x47.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-768x122.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/12-1024x162.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1302px) 100vw, 1302px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Modify the registry to turn off the Windows Defender function</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25876\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1312\" height=\"698\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13.png 1312w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-300x160.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-768x409.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/13-1024x545.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1312px) 100vw, 1312px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Call powershell to turn off Windows Defender</p>\n<p>SilentCleanup in the scheduled task can be started with normal user rights, and will be automatically elevated to high rights after startup. Based on this feature, this virus variant uses SilentCleanup, which has less strict permission control in scheduled tasks, to bypass user account control UAC.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/14.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25880\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/14.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1322\" height=\"358\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/14.png 1322w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/14-300x81.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/14-768x208.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/14-1024x277.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1322px) 100vw, 1322px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Virus variants use SilentCleanup to bypass UAC</p>\n<p>The virus will copy the zeVrk.exe file responsible for file encryption tasks to %LocalAppData%, %temp% and the Startup directory at startup, and add the zeVrk.exe file path to the registry startup key to achieve local persistence of encrypted ransomware , To achieve the purpose of scanning the disk again to encrypt new files when the user restarts the computer.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25884\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1314\" height=\"922\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15.png 1314w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15-300x211.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15-768x539.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/15-1024x719.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1314px) 100vw, 1314px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">The directory where zeVrk.exe (original file name) is located</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25888\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1320\" height=\"366\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16.png 1320w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-300x83.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-768x213.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/16-1024x284.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1320px) 100vw, 1320px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Registry startup items added by virus variants</p>\n<p>At the same time, in order to prevent the recovery of encrypted files, the virus variant will delete the disk volume shadow backup through the following commands, modify the startup policy to disable Windows startup repair, and delete the windows server backup backup:</p>\n<p>vssadmin delete shadows /all /quiet</p>\n<p>wmic shadowcopy delete</p>\n<p>bcdedit /set {default} bootstatuspolicy ignoreallfailures</p>\n<p>bcdedit /set {default} recoveryenabled no</p>\n<p>wbadmin delete catalog -quietIn the process of encrypting files, the exe program that is decrypted and loaded from the AndroidStudio.dll resource section will be responsible for the substantial encryption task, and its functions include: file occupation release, &#8220;RSA+AES&#8221; algorithm encryption, etc.</p>\n<p>The ransomware variant first enumerates the current processes through process snapshots, and through process name matching, ends more than 40 processes that may cause file occupation and affect encryption.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/17.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25892\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/17.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1316\" height=\"728\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/17.png 1316w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/17-300x166.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/17-768x425.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/17-1024x566.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1316px) 100vw, 1316px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The virus variant ends the specified process and releases the file occupation</p>\n<p>The Trojan will then scan the network shared disk and local disk of the current machine and prepare for file encryption.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/18.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25896\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/18.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"505\" height=\"275\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/18.png 505w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/18-300x163.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 505px) 100vw, 505px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/19.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25900\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/19.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"414\" height=\"250\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/19.png 414w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/19-300x181.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 414px) 100vw, 414px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The virus uses the AES256 algorithm to generate 32-byte AES keys for network shared disks and local disks. However, only the first 16 bytes of the key are random values obtained by the time factor and the SHA256 digest algorithm, and the last 16 bytes are taken from the 17-32 bytes of the attacker&#8217;s RSA public key built into the virus.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/20.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25904\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/20.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"510\" height=\"137\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/20.png 510w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/20-300x81.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 510px) 100vw, 510px\" /></a></p>\n<p>For the generated 32-byte AES key, the virus uses the RSA algorithm to encrypt it. The encrypted content includes the AES key, disk serial number, pseudo-random number, etc., a total of 128 bytes.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/21.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25908\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/21.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"713\" height=\"397\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/21.png 713w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/21-300x167.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Before starting file encryption, the virus first determines the size of the file to be encrypted. If the file is smaller than 0x180000 bytes (ie 1.5Mb) or the file to be encrypted is marked as a fully encrypted file type, phobos will encrypt all the file to be encrypted; otherwise, only part of the file is encrypted.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/22.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25912\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/22.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"750\" height=\"366\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/22.png 750w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/22-300x146.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Determine file size difference encryption method</p>\n<p>For fully encrypted files, the virus variant first creates a new file and splices the original file name with a specific suffix of the encrypted file. Then read the file data to be encrypted to the memory in sequence, use the AES random key and a 16-byte random initial variable to encrypt in CBC mode, and write the encrypted content to the newly created file in sequence.</p>\n<p>After the file data is encrypted, it will append the key, the original file and other related data to the end of the new file, a total of 0xF0 bytes. The end of the file mainly contains the following contents: 64 bytes including the encrypted original file name, AES encryption initial vector IV, the AES encryption key that has been RSA-encrypted and the system disk serial number, the 4-byte tail space size mark (0xF0), and the 6-byte constant value that is suspected to mark the version number of the Phobos virus.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/23.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25916\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/23.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"691\" height=\"572\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/23.png 691w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/23-300x248.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 691px) 100vw, 691px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/24.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25920\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/24.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"889\" height=\"248\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/24.png 889w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/24-300x84.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/24-768x214.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 889px) 100vw, 889px\" /></a></p>\n<p>For partially encrypted files, the virus reads data fragments with a size of 0x40000 bytes from the file to be encrypted 3 times, plus a constant and check value, uses the same encryption algorithm as full encryption for data encryption, and then writes the encrypted data to At the end of the file, the encrypted original data fragment is cleared.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/25.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25924\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/25.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"657\" height=\"617\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/25.png 657w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/25-300x282.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 657px) 100vw, 657px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Security advice</p>\n<p>1. Go to http://www.360totalsecurity.com/to download and install 360 Total Security, and keep the 360 Total Security process permanent, which can effectively protect against similar virus threats and prevent problems before they occur;</p>\n<p>2. Improve personal network security awareness and not easily download so-called &#8220;free&#8221; activation tools and other software from various download sites. It is recommended to download and install software from official channels. For unfamiliar software blocked by 360 Total Security, do not continue to run and add trust.</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>Md5:</p>\n<p>01f6d86a3e0050cb116ad4f16f12a420</p>\n<p>1e9d15d0e69d2ddaa1201eeb9859645e</p>\n<p>7f572cad5b68d5b32e330aca579152ae</p>\n<p>1c4e0d89e074f8fd8190a3887c378ed9</p>\n<p>f4b5c1ebf4966256f52c4c4ceae87fb1</p>\n<p>ac5f2c74c8c86f4c6914e646cf7ae975</p>\n<p>9e6b25770a41c39721dd3753e7924697</p>\n<p>636a3d5759907f7a3261beac3f75ca6a</p>\n<p>89cae80db18a87076fb59c2deff65b66</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>URLs:</p>\n<p>hxxp://boundertime.ru/pps.ps1</p>\n<p>hxxp://marcakass.ug/ac.exe</p>\n<p>hxxp://marcakass.ug/rc.exe</p>\n<p>hxxp://marcakass.ug/ds1.exe</p>\n<p>hxxp://marcakass.ug/ds2.exe</p>\n<p>hxxp://evanhopping.com/Zbixrpx.exe</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>The _f1d597afcb736a4e.webp","https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/23.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn59@2020_6/2020/08/25/02-18-21-638_c43bdde9847eb282.webp","https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/24.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn80@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-18-21-810_45ea8f89b0f50478.webp","https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/25.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn71@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-18-21-875_c3c0b8b60c780d9a.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598321894586},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 10:18:14","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 10:18:14","title":"Tor2Mine Revived Monero mining activity，360 Security Center has achieved comprehensive killing","link":"https://blog.360totalsecurity.com/?p=25248","description":"<img width=\"300\" height=\"158\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Тема-300x158.jpg\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium wp-post-image\" alt=\"title\" style=\"height: auto; max-width: 300px; width: 100%; margin-bottom: 20px;\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Тема-300x158.jpg 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Тема-768x403.jpg 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Тема-1024x538.jpg 1024w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Тема.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" /><p>With the substantial increase in the cost of mining Bitcoin, Monero has become a new trend, attracting many profit-making gangs. Recently, 360 Security Center monitoring found that Tor2Mine, a cryptocurrency mining organization active in 2018, has been unable to suppress itself. It has made a comeback with ambitions and controlled a large number of equipment through the spread of mining Trojans and other means, and organized Monero coin mining activity.</p>\n<p>According to 360 Security Center monitoring data, Tor2Mine is extremely good at disguising, and users are unknowingly reduced to mining &#8220;black labor&#8221;, and many countries such as Russia, Turkey, Spain, and Egypt have suffered.</p>\n<p>However, users need not worry too much, With the extreme intelligence of the 360 Security Center, 360 Total Security can strongly intercept and kill the Tor2Mine mining Trojan to protect the network security.</p>\n<p><strong>The download site becomes a &#8220;Tibetan Poison Station&#8221;, with a &#8220;surprise&#8221; when it is opened.</strong></p>\n<p>According to 360 Security Center monitoring, Tor2Mine started from &#8220;heart&#8221; this time,  hidden the mother program containing Trojan horse virus in some download site, using the existing user&#8217;s trust to deceive the download operation, which is equivalent to Turn on the &#8220;stolen&#8221; mode yourself Without guard.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25252\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"859\" height=\"200\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/1.png 859w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/1-300x70.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/1-768x179.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 859px) 100vw, 859px\" /></a></p>\n<p>(Download the running Trojan horse program from some download site)</p>\n<p>After the start of the operation, Tor2Mine&#8217;s ambitions were highlighted. The mining Trojan quickly resident and occupied the user&#8217;s computer by creating a scheduled task, but this is not the &#8220;end&#8221; of the story. It will also spread horizontally, which is really undesirable.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25256\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"727\" height=\"303\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/2.png 727w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/2-300x125.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 727px) 100vw, 727px\" /></a></p>\n<p>(After the Trojan horse program is running, it will reside in the infected machine through scheduled tasks and other methods)</p>\n<p>After an in-depth analysis of 360 Security Center, it is found that the means of &#8220;accumulating wealth&#8221; after its invasion are mainly divided into the following steps:</p>\n<p><strong>The first step: bypass the security software and clean up the &#8220;blocker&#8221;</strong></p>\n<p>After hacking the user&#8217;s computer, the mining Trojan will run a powershell code as the XMRigCC mining program loader. This operation can first determine whether the current process authority belongs to the administrator group, and further determine whether to shut down security software according to the authority, and the creation of mining related services.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25260\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"636\" height=\"122\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/3.png 636w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/3-300x58.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 636px) 100vw, 636px\" /></a></p>\n<p>(Tor2Mine permission judgment and preferences)</p>\n<p>If you have the administrator group permission, the Trojan loader adds the execution path of the mining program as the excluded file path of the Windows Defender scheduled scan and real-time scan, and closes the Windows Defender, sophos, Hitman anti-soft process.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25264\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"828\" height=\"334\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/4.png 828w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/4-300x121.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/4-768x310.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 828px) 100vw, 828px\" /></a></p>\n<p>(Tor2Mine against security software)</p>\n<p>Of course, this operations will also set PowerShell preferences to ignore warnings and errors and continue to execute silently, making its &#8220;trajectory of action&#8221; more concealed, so that it can be &#8220;a big fight&#8221;.</p>\n<p><strong>Step 2: Create scheduled tasks and services, get ready, &#8220;mining tool&#8221;</strong></p>\n<p>The Trojan Loader will firstly try to clean up the old services and mining programs that may exist, and then download and replace the original java.exe/javaw.exe as the main mining body. This program is a variant of XMRigCC, and Monero (XMR) The mining pool &#8220;eu.minerpool.pw:443&#8221; communicates.</p>\n<p>Then, the Trojan Loader will also create multiple scheduled tasks and services, all used to run the mining program java.exe/javaw.exe, and communicate with the dark web server through the tor2web service. In this way, the user quietly becomes a mining Mine broiler.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25268\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/5.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1297\" height=\"386\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/5.png 1297w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/5-300x89.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/5-768x229.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/5-1024x305.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1297px) 100vw, 1297px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">(Scheduled task and service name created by Tor2Mine)</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/6.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25272\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"517\" height=\"610\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/6.png 517w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/6-254x300.png 254w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 517px) 100vw, 517px\" /></a></p>\n<p>(Tumoruo coin mining pool address and login name and other information)</p>\n<p><strong>Step 3: anti-monitoring and horizontal penetration, wantonly &#8220;accumulate wealth&#8221;</strong></p>\n<p>After registering the scheduled tasks for mining, the mining Trojan will download del.ps1 from the server and try to close taskmgr&#8221;, &#8220;perfmon&#8221;, &#8220;SystemExplorer&#8221;, &#8220;taskman&#8221;, &#8220;ProcessHacker&#8221;, &#8220;procexp64&#8221;, &#8220;procexp&#8221; , &#8220;Procmon&#8221;, &#8220;Daphne&#8221; and other monitoring software processes; download ichigo-lite.ps1 to call Invoke-PowerDump (obtain administrator rights), Invoke-WMIExec, Invoke-TheHash (WMI horizontal movement) through the github open source project, So as to achieve the purpose of lateral penetration and loading and running again.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/7.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25276\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/7.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1356\" height=\"141\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/7.png 1356w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/7-300x31.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/7-768x80.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/7-1024x106.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1356px) 100vw, 1356px\" /></a></p>\n<p>(Tor2Mine uses open source projects to penetrate horizontally)</p>\n<p>It is worth mentioning that in the masked code of Tor2Mine, you can also find the code that uses the password grabbing artifact Mimikatz to obtain user credentials for horizontal penetration, which is equivalent to using the &#8220;acquaintance&#8221; identity pit &#8220;acquaintance&#8221;, which is unpredictable .</p>\n<p>The monitoring data of 360 Security Center also shows that since March 13th, the Tor2Mine mining program has grown significantly, indicating that the Tor2Mine mining program has achieved viral transmission through lateral penetration and controls a large number of devices.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/8.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25280\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/8.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1021\" height=\"143\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/8.png 1021w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/8-300x42.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/8-768x108.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1021px) 100vw, 1021px\" /></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">(Tor2Mine uses Mimikatz to penetrate horizontally)</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/9.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25284\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/9.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"785\" height=\"249\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/9.png 785w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/9-300x95.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/9-768x244.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 785px) 100vw, 785px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Tor2Mine mining program growth trend chart</p>\n<p>With the rapid development of science and technology, top-equipped equipment is sought after by users, but it is also easy to be the target of attack. Especially for these mining trojan horses that are good at invisible latent mining, their lethality cannot be underestimated. The &#8220;adversary&#8221;, while the computer is reduced to mining &#8220;black labor&#8221;, will also increase hardware losses. Therefore, the majority of users should increase their awareness of the prevention of such mining Trojans and protect their network security.</p>\n<p>Finally, for the mining Trojan that occupies computer resources, 360 Security Center provides the following security suggestions:</p>\n<ol>\n<li>Download and install 360 Total Security to effectively intercept such mining Trojan threats;</li>\n<li>Turn on 360 Total Security&#8217;s &#8221; Internet protection- Malicious Website Blocking&#8221;, identify various types of false fraudulent webpages, and block phishing websites and dangerous links.</li>\n<li>If it is found that the system resource consumption is abnormally high, it is necessary to consider the possibility of the operation of the mining Trojan, and use 360 Total Security to conduct a physical examination scan in time to check and kill the virus Trojan;</li>\n<li>Set the access rights of related servers/workstations to avoid the horizontal spread of Trojans;</li>\n<li>To enhance security awareness, it is recommended to download the software from official channels.</li>\n</ol>\n<p><a
