300px\" /><p>Starting in April this year, 360 Baize Lab intercepted a large number of attack samples from an unknown hacker organization. The hacker organization sent a phishing email to the victim by forging a police station investigation letter, COVID-19 detection notice, etc. , Through the backdoor virus to control the victim&#8217;s machine, steal valuable sensitive data related to the target.</p>\n<p>The PDB path of the virus samples used by the organization points to a user named &#8220;Vendetta&#8221;, and we will later also name the hacker organization Vendetta:</p>\n<p>“C:\\Users\\<strong>Vendetta</strong>\\source\\repos\\{project name}\\*\\obj\\Debug\\{project name}.pdb”</p>\n<p>In some samples, we have repeatedly detected the following tags, the virus author claims that he is from Italy:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.1.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25108\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"355\" height=\"55\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.1.png 355w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.1-300x46.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 355px) 100vw, 355px\" /></a></p>\n<p>However, we found in the naming of virus samples that virus authors like to use certain Turkish names to name variables, such as &#8220;RoboSki&#8221;, so we suspect that the organization originated in Europe:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.2.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25112\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"658\" height=\"275\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.2.png 658w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.2-300x125.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 658px) 100vw, 658px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Vendetta is a hacker organization that is very good at using social engineering. They forge phishing emails very realistically. They can easily gain users&#8217; trust and guide users to open the malicious programs they carry.</p>\n<p>The picture below is a Vendetta forgery of the investigation letter issued by the Austrian Federal Ministry of the Interior (BMI)</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25116\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"755\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.3.png 755w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.3-210x300.png 210w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.3-716x1024.png 716w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 755px) 100vw, 755px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Forged investigation letter from the Romanian police station:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.4.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25120\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1236\" height=\"812\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.4.png 1236w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.4-300x197.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.4-768x505.png 768w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.4-1024x673.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1236px) 100vw, 1236px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Forged the COVID-19 virus test email issued by the Australian Government Department of Health. The following figure is the code logic to extract the available pixel data and decrypt the shellcode:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.10.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25144\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.10.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"508\" height=\"646\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.10.png 508w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.10-236x300.png 236w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 508px) 100vw, 508px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>ReZer0</strong></p>\n<p>The execution logic of ReZer0 is controlled by hard-coded built-in instructions. According to different instructions, different malicious functions are executed. Its design logic resembles the design method of backdoor programs:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.11.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25148\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.11.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"698\" height=\"717\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.11.png 698w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.11-292x300.png 292w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 698px) 100vw, 698px\" /></a></p>\n<p>We have sorted out the hard-coded instructions and their corresponding meanings, most of which are not used:</p>\n<table width=\"0\">\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td width=\"92\"><strong>Hardcode[x]</strong></td>\n<td width=\"483\"><strong>Description</strong></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td rowspan=\"2\">0</td>\n<td>[0] == 4 load the plugin from the resource into memory</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>[0]! = 4 Inject the plugin in the resource into the system process to execute</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>1</td>\n<td>Whether to register scheduled tasks</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>4</td>\n<td>Download and execute any file</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>5</td>\n<td>Download file URL</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>6</td>\n<td>The execution path of the downloaded file</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>7</td>\n<td>Whether to detect the virtual machine</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>8</td>\n<td>Whether to detect sandbox</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>9</td>\n<td>ByPass antivirus software</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>29</td>\n<td>Show file version</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>34</td>\n<td>Sleep()</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>35</td>\n<td>Sleep duration</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody>\n</table>\n<p>In the 360 massive data, we found that ReZer0 has an obvious version identification. In conjunction with the above-mentioned large number of instructions used, we speculate that the software is still in the development stage, and it will not be ruled out that the program will be controlled through network communication in the future:</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.12.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-25152\" src=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.12.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"845\" height=\"648\" srcset=\"https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.12.png 845w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.12-300x230.png 300w, https://static.ts.360.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/514.12-768x589.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 845px) 100vw, 845px\" /></a></p>\n<p>In addition to the nature of the backdoor virus, ReZer0 also carries known remote control Trojans such as NanoCore and Remcos in the resources.
